SELECT ttype.*, c.*, field_title.fieldId as `content.title.id`,field_title.string as `content.title.string`, f.lang as `field.lang`, f.field as `field.field` FROM content c
				LEFT JOIN fields f ON c.contentId = f.contentId INNER JOIN pages ttype ON ttype.contentId = c.contentId
LEFT JOIN plugin_string field_title ON field_title.fieldId=f.id
				WHERE c.contentId=?
